<td style="text-align:center;">&#65518;</td>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;">&#65519;</td>
</tr>
</table>


**代码**

<pre class="line-numbers" data-start="0"><code class="language-bash"># Language: bash
	awk ''BEGIN{
	print "|||\n+------------------------------+"
	
	printf "=: #"
	for(j=0; j<=9; j++) printf ":=: %02d ", j
	print ":="
		for(i=0; i<=17370; i++) {
		if(i<6560 || i >13090) {
			printf "|%5d", i
			for(j=0; j<=9; j++) {
				N=10*i+j
				printf "|&#" N ";" 
			}
			print "|"
		}
		}
		
		print "+------------------------------+"
	}' >UTF-8.md
</code></pre>


**其他资料**

- [特殊符号](http://tw.piliapp.com/symbol/)
- [HTML Unicode (UTF-8) Reference](http://www.w3schools.com/charsets/ref_html_utf8.asp)
